inner join pr_resh on pr_resh.PERSNUM = pr_resh2.PERSNUM) pr_resh2
left join (Select pr_p.*, c_pr_p from pr_p
inner join (Select persnum,count(*) c_pr_p from pr_p group by PERSNUM) pr_p1 on pr_p.persnum = pr_p1.persnum) pr_p2 on pr_p2.persnum = pr_resh2.persnum

, P.ID_PROCESS

LEFT JOIN DB2ADMIN.TYPE_PROCESS AS TP ON TP.ID_TYPE_PROCESS=P.ID_TYPE_PROCESS
LEFT JOIN DB2ADMIN.C_UPFR AS KL ON KL.ID=P.ID_DEPARTMENT
WHERE T_OV.DATEOFCOMPLATION is not null),
pr_p as (
Select pr.id_process,pgi1.PERSNUM,pr.DATEOFCOMMING,pr.DATEOFCOMPLETION,pr.id_status from (Select id_process,P1.DATEOFCOMMING,P1.DATEOFCOMPLETION,p1.id_status from db2admin.processes p1 where p1.id_status<>4 and
exists (Select 1 from db2admin.type_process tp where tp.DESCRIPTION_PROCESS = 'Переплата' and p1.id_type_process = tp.id_type_process)) pr
inner join db2admin.PROCESS_GENERAL_INFO pgi1 on pgi1.ID_PROCESS = pr.id_process --where pr.DATEOFCOMMING >=
)

pr_p2.id_process id_process1,pr_p2.DATEOFCOMMING DATEOFCOMMING1,pr_p2.DATEOFCOMPLETION DATEOFCOMPLETION1
,pr_p2.id_status id_status1,pr_p2.c_pr_p from (Select pr_resh.*,pr_resh2.c_pr_resh from (Select PERSNUM,count(*) c_pr_resh from pr_resh group by PERSNUM) pr_resh2
inner join pr_resh on pr_resh.PERSNUM = pr_resh2.PERSNUM) pr_resh2
left join (Select pr_p.*, c_pr_p from pr_p
inner join (Select persnum,count(*) c_pr_p from pr_p group by PERSNUM) pr_p1 on pr_p.persnum = pr_p1.persnum) pr_p2 on pr_p2.persnum = pr_resh2.persnum
where (c_pr_resh<>c_pr_p or pr_p2.DATEOFCOMMING<pr_resh2.DATEOFCOMMING or pr_p2.DATEOFCOMMING is null or pr_resh2.DATEOFCOMMING is null )
